# 부록 C — 기능 상태와 추적 상세 참조

각 행은 기능의 상태뿐 아니라 활성화 경로, 권위, 의존성, 문법·진단·술어·예제 결합과 설명을 함께 보인다. `NOT_RUN`은 설계 또는 정적 자료가 제품 구현 증거를 대신하지 않는다는 뜻이다.

| `inout_borrow_move_modes`<br>move/borrow/inout mode surface | `canonical_feature`<br>활성화: `none`<br>권위: LANGUAGE / TYPE_SYSTEM | 없음 | 문법: `CaptureItem`, `ExpressionPrefixParselet`, `ParameterMode`<br>진단: `OWNERSHIP_MODE_ADMISSION_FAILED`<br>술어: `OwnershipModeAdmitted`<br>예제: `EX-R51a1-059`, `EX-R51a1-NG-072` | Parameter and capture modes are explicit. An ordinary \`mut name: T\` parameter acquires its argument once and commits a callee-owned mutable local: it creates no caller alias or write-back edge, and a failure before commit retains the caller owner. \`inout\` instead borrows one caller place exclusively for the dynamic call extent and successful writes remain visible in that place. borrow creates a nonescaping shared region view; move transfers ownership and invalidates the source. The narrow Stable profile permits replacement through an inout place but not moving the current value out of that borrowed place; definite reinitialization across every exit is not a current feature. Overlapping inout/borrow conflicts, use-after-move, escape across return/storage/capture, and crossing suspension or actor transfer without an admitted ownership proof are rejected.<br>제품: `NOT_RUN` |
